<tr><td width="742"><h3><a href="https://github.com/bgpzwe3866/djy/blob/master/gb/21/6/24/n13043851.md#1" target="_blank">连续10个月攀升 南加中位房价接近67万</a><br></h3><a href="https://github.com/bgpzwe3866/djy/blob/master/gb/21/6/24/n13043851.md#1" target="_blank"><img width="150" src="https://i.epochtimes.com/assets/uploads/2021/06/id13043863-shutterstock_547063339-1-150x120.jpg" align ="left"></a>在过去10个月内，南加州的房价中位价一直以两位数的速度快速攀升。热情的购房者，打破了过去的各种购房纪录。
